  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_339d329b-605c-4907-899d-22047065f844'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {

  <span id="freeText2367992125697044923" style="display:none">FORBIDDEN TEMPTATIONS <br /><br />Serena Kelley is an archaeologist and treasure hunter-and a woman with a secret. Since she was seven, she's been the keeper of a powerful charm that grants her health and immortality . . . as long as she stays a virgin. But Serena isn't all that innocent. And when a dangerously handsome stranger brings her to the brink of ecstasy, she wonders if she's finally met the one man she cannot resist. <br /><br />FATAL DESIRES <br /><br />Wraith is a Seminus demon with a death wish. But when an old enemy poisons him, he must find Serena and persuade her to give him the only known antidote in the universe-her charm. Yet, as she begins to surrender to his seductions and Wraith senses the cure is within his grasp, he realizes a horrible truth: He's falling for the woman whose life he must take in order to save his own.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1726186706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16454253029998682863"><b>
  <i>“All I ever had before you was nightmares. But now I dream. Because of you.”</i>
</b><br/><br/><br/>YES!!! I LOVED THIS BOOK!<br/><br/>This was utterly sensational! I have no idea why it took me so long to pick it up. Passion Unleashed is the third installment in Demonica series and it was so much better than the previous one. Just when I thought Eidolon is the most adorable among his brothers, Wraith proved me otherwise. Who would have thought a super bad boy like him could be such a sweetheart!? After seeing his soft and s</span>
  <span id="freeText16454253029998682863" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“All I ever had before you was nightmares. But now I dream. Because of you.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />YES!!! I LOVED THIS BOOK!<br /><br />This was utterly sensational! I have no idea why it took me so long to pick it up. Passion Unleashed is the third installment in Demonica series and it was so much better than the previous one. Just when I thought Eidolon is the most adorable among his brothers, Wraith proved me otherwise. Who would have thought a super bad boy like him could be such a sweetheart!? After seeing his soft and sweet side, I couldn’t help but fall in love with this demon!<br /><br />Wraith is a half vampire half Seminus demon. He was shot by the assassin with a poison dart, which slowly killed his libido. There was no cure and he was going to die. There was only one way to save his life, he needed to take a charm from a Marked Sentinel, and the way to get it was that he had to seduce the owner and had willing sex with her because the charm could only be transferred through sex.<br /><br />Serena is a Marked Sentinel. She'd been protected by a divine charm in order to keep the necklace, Heofon, safe. As long as she was still charmed, nothing could harm her against her will. If she lost her virginity, she would lose her charm too. For the fact that she was bitten by a Mara before she was charmed, and since there was no cure for Mara poison, as soon as her charm was taken away, the disease would advance rapidly and she would finally die.<br /><br />All Wraith's life, he only cared about himself. He put himself in some serious situation several times just for fun and did many horrible things without caring about the consequences. But since he met Serena, something happened inside of him. She made him see life differently. The way she made him feel, made him laugh, made him realize how wonderful it was to love and to be loved, was the thing he’d never experienced before. So this was the hardest decision he had to make, to choose between his life and hers. However, the time was almost out. If he didn't take her charm, with the brotherly bond, not only he would die but also his brothers.<br /><br />But when Serena was in great danger from the most deadly and powerful fallen angel, he swore he would protect her no matter what it cost him.<br /><br />As a fan of paranormal romance stories, I can undoubtedly say that this book totally hit the spot for me. I felt so overwhelmed while reading those scenes where the characters willingly sacrifice themselves in an attempt to save the lives of others. Those moments truly touched my heart. There were also some emotional moments that made me get a little teary-eyed. Moreover, all the plot twists were so darn brilliant, completely surprised me!<br /><br />If I could, I would definitely rate this book more than 5 stars! Thoroughly loved it!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16454253029998682863" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_40404743" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/40404743" />
    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/40404743?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal romance fans and wicked bad boy demon lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=pnr-angeldemon-fae-magic-witch-misc">pnr-angeldemon-fae-magic-witch-misc</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-player-manwhore-sex-addict">hero-player-manwhore-sex-addict</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-kickass-spirited-strong">heroine-kickass-spirited-strong</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=a-all-time-favorite-hero">a-all-time-favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-alpha">hero-alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=i-read-own-faves-keepers">i-read-own-faves-keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-na%C3%AFve-virgin-like-a-virgin">heroine-naïve-virgin-like-a-virgin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=pnr-vampires">pnr-vampires</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40404743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12028486535683133505">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br/><br/>Reading Passion Unleashed, I found myself once again transported to Ione’s sinfully decadent, wickedly dark, and utterly imaginative world of the Demonica with its diverse demon species, fallen angels, vampires, weres/wargs, werebeasts, shifters, slayers, humans, and half-breeds fighting for coexistence and peace. I’m continually blown away by Ione’s brilliance and creativity as a writer and the series just keeps getting better and better. Ione's writing is fresh, in</span>
  <span id="freeText12028486535683133505" style="display:none">5+ stars – Paranormal Romance<br /><br />Reading Passion Unleashed, I found myself once again transported to Ione’s sinfully decadent, wickedly dark, and utterly imaginative world of the Demonica with its diverse demon species, fallen angels, vampires, weres/wargs, werebeasts, shifters, slayers, humans, and half-breeds fighting for coexistence and peace. I’m continually blown away by Ione’s brilliance and creativity as a writer and the series just keeps getting better and better. Ione's writing is fresh, inventive, witty, and intelligent, the characters are sexy, original, and genuine, and the story is hypnotic and full of sizzling sensuality and dark humor.<br /><br />I love level-headed Eidolon and smooth-as-silk Shade, but devil-may-care bad boy Wraith has always been my favorite of the Seminus Demon brothers, so Passion Unleashed is definitely my favorite in the series so far. <br /><br />In Passion Unleashed, Wraith has been poisoned by an assassin and the only cure is to obtain a charm from spunky, inquisitive, spirited, independent archaeologist Serena. The charm/cure happens to be Serena’s virginity, and she’s pretty darn determined to hold onto it, despite Wraith’s smooth attempts at seduction, since she seals her own fate if she loses it. Wraith’s destiny is tied to Underworld General hospital and his brothers, so as he dies from the poison, UG deteriorates and his brothers’ lives are also at stake, which makes his choice to take Serena’s “charm” even more difficult. <br /><br />The plot involves forces of good and evil engaging in the ultimate apocalyptic battle for the future of all races, which is also tied to Serena’s charm. Kynan and Gem’s relationship plays an important role in the story, as does the fallen angel Reaver, malevolent villain Byzamoth, and a new character, Lore, who will probably have his story told in the next book in the series.<br /><br />Serena is a great heroine, loads of fun (sort of like a blonde, virginal Lara Croft), and her chemistry and banter with Wraith is delectable. Wraith has been a blast from the beginning of the series because he’s charismatic, wicked, funny, cocky, arrogant, honest, and lives for only hunting, fighting, and sex. Tortured bad boy heroes are always the most passionate and surprising because when they finally fall, they fall fast, hard, and completely, and Wraith is no exception. Wraith’s transformation and growth from an emotionally distant, reckless, pissed-off-at-the-whole-world, I-don’t-give-a-crap-about-anyone-but-myself, hedonistic bad boy personality to attentive, tender, caring, generous, protective, and affectionate lover is sweet, touching, and funny. Wraith and Serena’s relationship is heartwarming and bittersweet, and the plot keeps you guessing until the very end as to how things will get resolved for the characters to find their HEA.<br /><br />The book has a Demonica Compendium in the back with all kinds of cool special content that makes for a kick-ass bonus.<br /><br />Ione is definitely a fresh voice in the paranormal romance genre and her talent as a writer is first-rate. The Demonica series truly stands out for its originality, unique characters, dark wit, scorching sensuality, and raw eroticism. Passion Unleashed is a spellbinding and sexy read...a well deserved 5+ stars.<br /><br />I’m eager for more of Ione's captivating, wicked hot saga, so I don’t know how I’m going to manage waiting almost an entire year before book four Ecstasy Unveiled comes out in February 2010!</span>
  <a data-text-id="12028486535683133505" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_47675715" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/47675715" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/47675715?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of complex paranormal romance/urban fantasy, supernatural fiction</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-redeems-himself">hero-redeems-himself</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=demon">demon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hero-or-heroine-gravely-ill">hero-or-heroine-gravely-ill</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=kickbutt-heroine">kickbutt-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hot-and-steamy-romance">hot-and-steamy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=owned-copy">owned-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer47675715" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4126925206451416334">This is one of those reviews where I have to admit I'm wrong. I didn't like Wraith at all before I read this book. I thought my feelings would be unlikely to change, even though I love this series, and Larissa Ione's writing. Well, I was dead wrong. There. I said it. I ended up loving Wraith. And I have no regrets.<br/><br/>Wraith is one of those heroes who snuck up on me. I think it was the sign of the high caliber of Ms. Ione's writing. Wraith is very in-your-face with his often unlikeable, selfish natu</span>
  <span id="freeText4126925206451416334" style="display:none">This is one of those reviews where I have to admit I'm wrong. I didn't like Wraith at all before I read this book. I thought my feelings would be unlikely to change, even though I love this series, and Larissa Ione's writing. Well, I was dead wrong. There. I said it. I ended up loving Wraith. And I have no regrets.<br /><br />Wraith is one of those heroes who snuck up on me. I think it was the sign of the high caliber of Ms. Ione's writing. Wraith is very in-your-face with his often unlikeable, selfish nature. But Ms. Ione employed a careful subtlety in crafting his story. I went into it thinking that he was callous and uncaring. But I came to realize that he had a massive defense mechanism going on. There are few people that have the power to make or break another person. And parents are at the top of the list. If someone goes bad, the first instinct is to say that he wasn't raised right. Well, that's not always true. But, I think it's very true in Wraith's case. His mother treated him like he was an abomination. I'm not saying that she doesn't have a reason to feel some bitterness about Wraith being forced on her by his Seminus demon father. But to treat a child the way she did was just plain wrong. It's no wonder that Wraith was lacking in moral character. He cared about his brothers, and killing vampires. Not much else, after that. Sex was important because a Seminus demon will die without it. But I don't even think that sex was all that important to him. It was something that he did to stay alive. To him, seducing females was a biological imperative. When he found out he had to seduce a virgin human woman in order to survive the toxin he had been poisoned with, that's when things got complicated. Because of the tortures his mother afflicted on him, Wraith stays far away from human females. But, he has no choice. And he's almost ready to say no to doing it, until he finds out that the hospital that his brothers and he built will fail if he dies, there's no getting out of this particular seduction.<br /><br />When Wraith and Serena meet, I could feel the chemistry, but Wraith is still in callous mode. I was still unconvinced of him as hero I could fall for. But slowly that starts to change as I saw how Wraith ended up loving Serena for who she was, how he protected her, and how he continually passed up on opportunities to do 'the deed'. And as I saw how tender his heart was, buried under many layers of scar tissue, I was seduced into softening my own heart to him. How he suffered as his body shut down, but wouldn't take Serena, knowing he'd cause her own demise. How he gave her pleasure without consummation, which contributed to his own agony. That was the mark of selfless love. By the end of this book, I was deeply in love with Wraith. In fact, he's my favorite brother up to this point.<br /><br />Serena's character was well-drawn as well. She had lived her life knowing she can never be fully intimate with a man, or she'll die. But she's managed to live a full, adventurous life, regardless of that. I liked her passion and her spirit. And her good heart. She was just the woman for Wraith.<br /><br />Another 'character' that took center stage was the awesome world-building and storytelling. Ms. Ione has this reader impressed. Her world is so rich and fascinating. The way she took this concept to the next level by incorporating fallen angels, one who longs to return to Heaven, and another who strives to bring Hell to Heaven and to rule over earth as a god. What a marked, fascinating conrast. The complexity of the demon species, and their interactions with each other. How very different they all are. In my mind, a demon is a demon. Not so in this series. In some ways this series has an intense, horrific vibe to it. Not that I'm complaining. I am a fan or horror, after all. She gets serious props with the way she's able to make me feel uneasy with some of the aspects of this story. And the action sequences were excellent, with smaller skirmishes and smack-downs, and full on epic battles. The characters get hurt, and sometimes mortally. The cost is higher than you can even imagine.<br /><br />The tension in this book is sustained, as you wonder how things will work out. In this dicey situation, success can only occur at the expense of someone else. Who will live? Who will die? You don't find out until almost the very end of the book. And things aren't wrapped up in a neat package. A sacrifice has to be made. But at the same time, I came out of this book very satisfied.<br /><br />It's hard to get everything into words, but I was thoroughly satisfied with this book. I was kept guessing what would happen, in a state of delightful suspense, as this book unfolds. I was completely entertained with the beautiful romance, fiery passion, the family dynamics, the incredibly interesting world-building and lore-spinning, and the grand adventure of it all. This was just a great book all-around. <br /><br />I can't wait to read Lore's story. I'm already in love with him!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4126925206451416334" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=nooo-way">nooo-way</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9752625-sandra?shelf=beautifully-written">beautifully-written</a>
          </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11248660598239725081"><b>Re-read from June 22nd-24th 2013</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText11248660598239725081" style="display:none"><b>Re-read from June 22nd-24th 2013</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749794.gif" alt="tumblr mjrxyitcjg1s2sfako1 500 zps26de3803" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Let's be clear on this," he growled. "You have no idea how badly I want to be inside you. Standing up, lying down, taking you from behind. All of it. Right now."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749795.gif" alt="35559 Jenna marbles panties throwing Ua SJ zpse16" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Reading <i>Passion Unleashed</i> (the 3rd book in the <i>Demonica </i>series) gave me the pleasure of loosing myself once again in the magnificent and awesome world <i>Larissa</i> has created. It's full of hot vampires, demons, werewolfs, fallen angels, shifters, slayers, and to sum it up everything you can imagine and want in a book like this one. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388925i/749796.jpg" alt="472341ab e09a 4e3c a134 178894a76d87 zps2a393936" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Wraith has been poisoned by an assassin and the only cure is to obtain a charm from spunky, inquisitive, spirited, independent archaeologist Serena. In order to do that he has to take Serena's virginity. Even when he senses the cure is within his reach when she begins to surrender, he realizes something - He's falling for someone who he needs to take away life from so he can save his own. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380388925i/749797.jpg" alt="f2e3ff18 4340 426b acdb 3e1bd1c901fd zpsf126963e" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Dear Eidolon and Shade, as much as i loved you guys, i'll have to ditch you for Wraith. Sorry. But he's the one! ;)<br><br>Larrisa Ione has a huge talent in writing. Her books are always captivating, action-packed and simply amazing. Her characters are always awesome, kick-ass and very likable. You can easily visualize what's happening because of her well done description. And you can get into the books with ease. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749798.gif" alt="tumblr lxibb4s Qkg1qhcwfso1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Why i loved Wraith?:</b>
</u> Man! There are so many reasons why i simply adored him. First of all...<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749799.gif" alt="tumblr m52cj9jx GV1qdr16ko1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749800.gif" alt="tumblr lml3zbf A6 O1qewlku" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>We know Wraith from book 1 &amp; 2, and we know him for causing disaster everywhere he goes, for his tragic past, and generally for being a bad boy like no other! <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>His voice was low and rough … “What about you? Do you like bad boys?”<br>“There’s definitely appeal,” she breathed. <br>“Good,” He bent and clipped her earlobe with his teeth … “Because they don’t come badder than me.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br> With characters like Wraith, when their dark side breaks their surface, watch out, because only a very special woman is going to be able to peal back these layers and find the tenderness inside. Wraith finds that special woman, but loving her comes with deadly consequences.<br><br><u>
  <b>Why i loved Serena?:</b>
</u> Serena isn't you typical virgin. She is bad! And i think that's what makes her and Wraith so perfect for each other. She isn't afraid to be herself. For example, she ain't gonna be drinkin' tea or water when she wants whiskey just because she's in the presence of a hot guy. That's my kinda girl!<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749801.gif" alt="tumblr m715ny JOk U1r3fk5s" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>And even if she's a virgin, she isn't one by choice. If she could, she would have lost it ages ago. Serena knows about sex, she hasn't got tons of experience (like 'duhh') but she isn't shy about it. And we all know that with Wraith helping her out? It won't be long until she'll become a sex goddess or something like that. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749802.gif" alt="tumblr m8rj5suqos1qga56po1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I'd drop one hand to your waist, but i don't know if i could be patient enough to unbutton your pants, or if i'd just rip them. Either way, i'd get in. I'd find that sweet place between your legs with my fingers, and i'd play until we were both panting. You'd be wet and ready for me when i dropped to my knees and replaced my hand with my mouth."</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I loved how Serena's kindness and enthusiasm brought the good in Wraith that was hidden somewhere underneath all that muscle *wink*. He changed from being selfish and careless, to actually being thoughtful, protective and loving. And i absolutely adored his development!<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749803.gif" alt="tumblr mje721 Bve T1qmd323o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“No. It was because it was the first time I made love to anyone. You can call me a liar or anything else, but do not doubt me on this. And I swear to you that you were the first, and you will be the last."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>The only thing that would make this book better was if we could read more about the previous characters and how they are doing (e.g Tayla&amp;Eidolon, Runa&amp;Shade). We did get glimpses of them, but for me it wasn't enough. <br><br><b>Overall </b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749804.gif" alt="5stars" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b><i>Passion Unleashed</i> was my first ever actuall re-read, and guess what?...</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380388925ra/749805.gif" alt="tumblr mbszwc2 Z8n1rsw1yf" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Wraith is definitely <b>my favorite</b> of the brothers, and his story is my fav as well. There is a lot more action, humor and kick-arsery. And the ending was adorable like always. I'll be re-reading the 4th book next, and i <b>recommend this series to everyone who hasn't read it yet</b>! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“All I ever had before you was nightmares. But now I dream. Because of you.” </b>
</blockquote></span>

    <a title="Julie (jjmachshev)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/882708-julie-jjmachshev"><img alt="Julie (jjmachshev)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1208126390p2/882708.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/39733224?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie (jjmachshev)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie (jjmachshev)" href="/user/show/882708-julie-jjmachshev">Julie (jjmachshev)</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/882708-julie-jjmachshev?shelf=2009-reads">2009-reads</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer39733224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4170190879409843487">YES! YES! YES! Excuse me, I'm having a private moment ;) I finished "Passion Unleashed" by Larissa Ione and I must say that this is one series I'm so very glad I'm hooked on. Her Demonica novels take place in an intricately built world, with enough differences from the raft of paranormals available to distinguish themselves. The characters are NOT one-dimensional caricatures of one creature or another...oh no, Ione has a vast selection of characters with multi-layered personalities on top of the</span>
  <span id="freeText4170190879409843487" style="display:none">YES! YES! YES! Excuse me, I'm having a private moment ;) I finished "Passion Unleashed" by Larissa Ione and I must say that this is one series I'm so very glad I'm hooked on. Her Demonica novels take place in an intricately built world, with enough differences from the raft of paranormals available to distinguish themselves. The characters are NOT one-dimensional caricatures of one creature or another...oh no, Ione has a vast selection of characters with multi-layered personalities on top of the traits attributable to their species and these differences from the average urban fantasy or paranormal romance today are just a couple of the things that make her novels stand-outs, IMHO :)<br /><br />In "Passion Unleashed" we finally get the story of Wraith, a sex demon who's 'gotta have it'! So 'have it' he does...often and with vigor. He's the 'bad boy' of the three brothers we've read about so far and Ione certainly puts him to the test in his love story. Wraith has been infected with a poison that has no antidote. He's only got one chance to save his life...find the 'Chosen' virgin and 'deflower' her. Hey! He's a sex demon--no problem.<br /><br />Serena is one of the 'Chosen'--she holds a relic that would be pivotal in the event of Armageddon. This same relic is all that protects her from an incurable disease she contracted at a young age. So holding on to her virginity isn't really a choice...it's the only thing keeping her alive. Good thing Armageddon isn't on the calendar, huh? Ummm, hold that thought. There's a fallen Angel turned renegade and he's after Serena's relic. So the chase...I mean race, is on. Oh, just one more thing. The fallen Angel can TAKE the relic from Serena, but Wraith will have to seduce it from her. But really, sex demon, no problem, right?<br /><br />I don't mean to make this book sound like a light-heated paranormal romance, because it's not. Although there is much more humor in this story than the previous two, it's still a nail-biter of a suspense/action novel. And Ione doesn't let the action/suspense overcome the love aspect either. Both Wraith and Serena face life and death decisions that will affect not just themselves, but their friends, loved ones, and heck...the whole world! No pressure.<br /><br />Others have reviewed "Passion Unleashed" and gone into more detail so I won't take up your time with more words. What I will say is that if you like urban fantasy, spicy paranormal romance, action and suspense, drama, and hot supernatural creatures...RUN, don't walk, to your nearest bookstore and pick up this whole series. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4170190879409843487" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17949834856539706317">^^I WANNA UNLEASH SOME PASSION ALRIGHT!^^<br/><br/>I know I am sounding like a broken record, but I am gonna say this again “everyone needs to read this series”. I am just always surprised and excited when I get into one these books, seems like the last book is always a bit better than the previous. This book, good gawd I was cheering, I cried, laughed, lost my pants all at the same time. I call that a fantastic read.<br/><br/>A little recap, this series is the Demonica series, and it revolves around a tight knit g</span>
  <span id="freeText17949834856539706317" style="display:none">^^I WANNA UNLEASH SOME PASSION ALRIGHT!^^<br /><br />I know I am sounding like a broken record, but I am gonna say this again “everyone needs to read this series”. I am just always surprised and excited when I get into one these books, seems like the last book is always a bit better than the previous. This book, good gawd I was cheering, I cried, laughed, lost my pants all at the same time. I call that a fantastic read.<br /><br />A little recap, this series is the Demonica series, and it revolves around a tight knit group of demons, the first three books have been about the sem bros (seminus demons) and they have been good. We had Dr E, Shade and now we have Wraith, and Wraith is the bad boy, he does what he wants, kills whom he wants and has sex with anything that moves and is a demon. Just a few simple rules, only females and no humans, he dislikes human females but his views are about to change, when the very species he hates, one will have the power to save his life.<br /><br />Wraith is the bad boy with the troubled past, he does everything for himself and don’t give a damn about nobody. Too bad, he can’t turn of the feelings for his brothers because they are the only one who seems to care about him. Trust comes a long way with Wraith, after the woman who birthed him kept him and tortured him, some mother she was. Therefore, Wraith is all types of assholish due to the emotional and physical pain his mom put him through. As a seminus demon, he is half-vampire and he hates that part of himself, because vampires were responsible for the most painful days of his life. So destroying a few vamps is never a bad thing for Wraith, but there are rules, vamps can’t destroy their own kind but rules were meant to be broken. Wraith breaks them and let me tell you he breaks them like a rockstar.<br /><br />When taking down a few bad vamps Wraith is attacked and infected a with a poison that there is no cure for, and will eventually shut down and kill his body in a matter of weeks. Thus, begins the search for a cure and what will save his life is the very thing he would give up his life for. Wraith needs to take a charm from a human female, that includes taking her virginity and this will not come easy but Wraith is up for the challenge because he don’t give a fuck about no one. WRONG!!!!! He will come to care he will come to love a lot.<br /><br />Serena Kelley is charmed, translation she is protected by strong magic. No harm can come to her; only thing is this is only good if she remains a virgin. That’s tough when all you wanna do is get butt naked with a hottie, but getting sentimental this means no intimacy or love for Serena. Only lover she has is her job, and when a most desired artifact is in reach, she makes her way to get it, she would have to meet Josh to receive a key and Josh is all kinds of heavenly with his face tats and blond hair. Never realizing that the Josh she is meeting is Wraith in disguise. Now every feeling is put on the test in close proximity to this walking Adonis. It also seems some crazy man wants her virginity and charm to bring destruction to the world. Good thing she has Josh (Wraith), and all he wants is to get to know her and protect her.<br /><br />This book is a plethora of information and if I go on it will be review to long to read, but I can’t go without talking about Wraith. I noticed him from the first book, because he is such an ass but I was not in love with him. Now, I am in love with him now he is the epitome of pure awesomeness. He loves fierce like how he kills; his heart is beautiful even though he can’t say it through words. I wanna be the Blob or a snake or something, so I can wrap myself around him and pull him into myself (psychotic much) he is bloody beautiful, he deserved every happiness he got and more. Also, I am convinced Wraith is a little bit gay no matter if he says otherwise, every comment he said was a little bit gay. He likes to talk about lubing up, calling someone daddy, what do you wanna kiss me, Wraith gay is definitely a very good thing.<br /><br />We got a little bit of everyone in this book, and all of Ione’s characters is never a bad thing. This woman can write and I want to live in her head. I liked Serena and she was the ying to Wraith’s yang. I am just so happy about how much she loved him he deserved it. The info around the charm was sweet and added something dynamite to the plot. It is a showdown everyone, a kickasss showdown.<br /> It has Angels, fallen angels, wolves, hot sex and more hot sex with a dash of hot sex. There is just so much that happens, I can't even think!<br /><br />This series is A+++++; I am in love with everyone. I am unsure of which bro is my fave is it Shade, is it Wraith I have no clue. I will say I am up for some tag teaming and I don’t care if I can’t walk, move or breathe after. It would be “alright” in my book.<br /><br />A BIG CHECK THIS SERIES OUT!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="17949834856539706317" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1371358791" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17361835939453299243">The story of Wraith and Serena is a mixture of a paranormal romance (Wraith is a vampire-Seminus demon) and an Indiana Jones archeological adventure (Serena is an archeologist-top adventurer-treasure hunter).<br/><br/>Wraith is the second brother of Eidolon. His upbringing was really tough. Thus, he has become emotional unstable, scarred inside, untrusting, badass. And of course a man-whore. All Seminus demons are like that in order to survive.<br/><br/>Serena has a secret since she was seven years old. She used to</span>
  <span id="freeText17361835939453299243" style="display:none">The story of Wraith and Serena is a mixture of a paranormal romance (Wraith is a vampire-Seminus demon) and an Indiana Jones archeological adventure (Serena is an archeologist-top adventurer-treasure hunter).<br /><br />Wraith is the second brother of Eidolon. His upbringing was really tough. Thus, he has become emotional unstable, scarred inside, untrusting, badass. And of course a man-whore. All Seminus demons are like that in order to survive.<br /><br />Serena has a secret since she was seven years old. She used to be a kid on the verge of death until she was given a charm, Heofon, by an angel which made her kind of immortal. Her immortality is connected to her virginity. As long as she is untouched, the illness will not come back and she will live forever.<br /><br />Unfortunately bad boy Wraith sets his eyes on her, since he learned that he needs her charm in order to survive. He has been poisoned by an assassin and his only survival is Serena’s charm. <br /><br />At the beginning, he will pose as her aid and he will help her with her adventures. Innocent Serena will be fascinated by him and she will be tempted. Seminus demons can be very persuasive and Wraith has also the advantage of visiting her dreams and making her see what she is missing. But Wraith will also be captivated by her. He will start finally caring for someone except himself. <br /><br />Serena is going to have the final say! But Wraith is so crazy in love with her that he will never let her die <br />– even if he has to bend some of his personal rules<br />- even if he has to beg<br /><br />It is great seeing the change in Wraith’s personality. It is awesome accompanying Wraith and Serena at their adventures. It is interesting to understand what is Heofon and guess who will have it in the end.<br /><br />Note: Gem &amp; Kynan's story occupies also a large proportion of the book. Gemella Endri aka Gem is half demon and the sister of Tayla. Kynan is one of the Aegis Elders (Aegis is the demon-hunters' organization). The development of their story will not be easy because Kynan is not fond of demons. </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠" href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed?shelf=demons">demons</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1435579640" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16933857370153128224">Ok, so 4 stars might be too high, but I'm astounded that I didn't hate the main characters, nor did they do anything to annoy me. See, astounding. <br/><br/>Story goes Wraith has been poisoned by an assassin with a poison to which there is no cure, except maybe this angelic charm worn by an Aegis human. The catch, if you care about people, is removing the charm from this specific person equals death for the human. Wraith is fine with that, until he meets the charmed human, Serena. Serena is an adventurer-</span>
  <span id="freeText16933857370153128224" style="display:none">Ok, so 4 stars might be too high, but I'm astounded that I didn't hate the main characters, nor did they do anything to annoy me. See, astounding. <br /><br />Story goes Wraith has been poisoned by an assassin with a poison to which there is no cure, except maybe this angelic charm worn by an Aegis human. The catch, if you care about people, is removing the charm from this specific person equals death for the human. Wraith is fine with that, until he meets the charmed human, Serena. Serena is an adventurer-archeologist and wears a charm that makes her invulnerable &amp; kind of immortal. The catch, she has to keep her purity to keep the charm, you know, the one keeping her from dying from an incurable disease. <br /><br />Wraith was the badass, mouthy, pain in the ass, uncaring, emotionally scarred &amp; unhinged, brother. He also hates humans and would be killing tons if the Vampire Council wouldn't punish him for it. He invests himself in Serena's search for ancient objects and he finds himself actually liking her, a human. It's interesting how kind and caring he is to her, all while protecting her from the multiple demons and villains coming after her. Serena, she's fascinated by Wraith and his hotness, but can't ride that pony. Instead she likes him for that other stuff, like his personality and good deeds. They're sweet together. They're also steamy together. <br /><br />I liked this book because of the character evolution Wraith goes through, the very evil villain Byzamoth (and his way with loopholes), the coming together of different factions, the whole adventure fueled plot, and the ending. The end hoo-rah was good and creative. The addition of Lore and Kynan was nice. <br /><br />Speaking of Kynan, the book is 80% Wraith's story, with the rest being Gem &amp; Kynan's story. Now I utterly loathed Gem to the depths of Sheoul in the previous two books, but she wasn't as bad in this book. I still loathe her and wish she'd be a causality, but she was minusculely less annoying in this book. Liked Kynan's part in the hoo-rah and his ending. <br /></span>

<div id="review_121622148" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/121622148" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/121622148?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2011-reads">2011-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=format-paperback">format-paperback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=curses">curses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-larissa-ione">author-larissa-ione</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-demonica-ione">series-demonica-ione</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=pnr-everything-but-the-kitchen-sink">pnr-everything-but-the-kitchen-sink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-completed">series-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=pnr-demons">pnr-demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer121622148" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5976985747679422913"><br/><i>Passion Unleashed</i> is another entertaining, exciting installment to the <i>Demonica</i> series, and while I did liked it, I didn’t love it.<br/><br/>I thought the story itself was great. Wraith has been poisoned and to save himself, he has to find a special charm, an amulet whose keeper is a human. He not only has to take the item from her, but he also has to take her virginity. <b>Slight Spoiler</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Now, if left at that, it sounds like a cheesy way to toss sex into the story, but it really worked for m</span></span>
  <span id="freeText5976985747679422913" style="display:none"><br /><i>Passion Unleashed</i> is another entertaining, exciting installment to the <i>Demonica</i> series, and while I did liked it, I didn’t love it.<br /><br />I thought the story itself was great. Wraith has been poisoned and to save himself, he has to find a special charm, an amulet whose keeper is a human. He not only has to take the item from her, but he also has to take her virginity. <b>Slight Spoiler</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Now, if left at that, it sounds like a cheesy way to toss sex into the story, but it really worked for me because the real edginess and emotional angst of the story comes in because Wraith’s brothers, Shade and Eidolin, are also affected, as well as UGH – Underground General Hospital – which is literally falling apart. The three of them are closely tied to the hospital, their combined powers protecting the building and those within, but the closer Wraith come to dying, the more unstable the building itself becomes,making it nearly impossible to treat patients and save lives. And if that’s not bad enough, if the keeper loses the amulet, she’ll die a slow, painful death.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> So how can Wraith possibly reconcile himself with what he has to do to stay alive and what will happen to the woman he’s fallen in love with if he does? I really enjoyed the ensuing dilemma, the drama, and the angst of the situation and thought the way it was all resolved was great!<br /><br />Throughout the first two books, <i>Pleasure Unbound</i> and <i>Desire Unchained,</i> I saw Wraith as this incredibly tortured soul who was so far gone he was nearly beyond redemption. Unfortunately, I didn’t get that same feeling in his book. Even though he was still rough and edgy, he seemed almost to be a watered down version of his earlier self. I kept waiting for the WOW to kick in, but it didn’t happen for me. <br /><br />The heroine, Serena Kelley, wasn’t someone I became totally invested in. Don’t get me wrong, I felt bad for what her life had become and was destined to remain, but for a character as a whole, I just didn’t connect on a truly deep level with her and I can’t put my finger on why.<br /><br />I was expecting this to be a five star read, but unfortunately it didn’t reach that level for me. I’m giving <i>Passion Unleashed</i> three stars because while I loved the storyline itself, I feel like almost anyone could have stepped into the role of hero and heroine.<br /><br />I'm looking forward to reading the next book in this series!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5976985747679422913" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer16170169604645022487">I'm totally loving this Demonica series. Larissa Ione writes with really creative world-building and awesome connection between her characters. I love the conflict brought up in each book and also the family connection between the Sem brothers. In this third book, Wraith is featured, and he has to figure out a way to get a charm away from Serena. The charm prevents the person who possesses it from being killed or dying, and the conflict is intense because Wraith has been cursed, so he's dying, a</span>
  <span id="freeText16170169604645022487" style="display:none">I'm totally loving this Demonica series. Larissa Ione writes with really creative world-building and awesome connection between her characters. I love the conflict brought up in each book and also the family connection between the Sem brothers. In this third book, Wraith is featured, and he has to figure out a way to get a charm away from Serena. The charm prevents the person who possesses it from being killed or dying, and the conflict is intense because Wraith has been cursed, so he's dying, and Serena had been given the charm in the firs place because SHE was dying. So, the only way to save himself is to kill her (which frankly, was the only part of the plot that sort of icked me out.) <br /><br />Wraith gets to be his usual vampire-y self, has lots of conflict with his brothers, and eventually he and Serena have to figure things out. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I enjoyed this one, even if it was a little strange seeing Serena call Wraith "Josh" for most of the book, and the part about having to take her virginity/charm to save himself meant killing her kind of made Wraith less heroic in my eyes. But for the most part, it was enjoyable. I always enjoy Ione's writing.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> 4.5/5 stars<br /><br />Please excuse typos/name misspellings. Entered on screen reader.</span>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">paranormal romance fans, especially girls who love a tortured hero</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer118066834" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2402273149268543425">Dear Eidolon, <br/><br/>As much as I loved you, I am leaving you for Wraith. Yes, he's stubborn and selfish and demented in a lot of ways, but he has passion as is evident in the title of his book. I'm sorry. Please don't kill me.<br/><br/>Love,<br/>me<br/><br/>Yup, it's true. I've found a new lover and his name is Wraith. I am absolutely spellbound by this book. It's probably my favourite so far, though I haven't been reading the series in order. There's still Shade's book (which I can't find) and Lore's book (which I have) to l</span>
  <span id="freeText2402273149268543425" style="display:none">Dear Eidolon, <br /><br />As much as I loved you, I am leaving you for Wraith. Yes, he's stubborn and selfish and demented in a lot of ways, but he has passion as is evident in the title of his book. I'm sorry. Please don't kill me.<br /><br />Love,<br />me<br /><br />Yup, it's true. I've found a new lover and his name is Wraith. I am absolutely spellbound by this book. It's probably my favourite so far, though I haven't been reading the series in order. There's still Shade's book (which I can't find) and Lore's book (which I have) to look forward to. If Passion Unleashed is any indication for what to expect, I am in for a real treat.<br /><br />I LOVED THIS BOOK! Truth is, I never wanted things to end. Everything was amazing. The plot, the romance, the writing. Superb. Did I really just use that word? I did, because it's the truth. <br /><br />As much as I loved Wraith and Serena, I must admit I found the thing between Kynan, Gem and Lore to be hilarious. I think my favourite thing about this book is the appearance of the middle finger. It always makes me smile because anger and hatred can be expressed with a single motion. And with so much testosterone in this book, it's bound to get a little crazy! <br /><br />Favourite Quote:<br />Speaking of which... the human from last night was standing near the ambulance bay doors, his gaze full of murder. So it was with great pleasure that Lore grasped Gem by her upper arm, pulled her around, and kissed her. <br />With tongue.<br />He kept his gaze locked on the human, and as he stepped back from Gem, he flipped the guy off. Cold rage burned in the male's eyes, as well as an unspoken threat that promised pain.<br />p.192<br /><br />5 STARS! </span>

  <span id="freeText17250012365752845029" style="display:none">SPOILERS<br />****I do believe I summarized it a bit, people, consider yourselves warned***<br /><br /><br /><br />My favorite so far. Not only did I love Wraith, but Serena was his perfect counterpart! And the celibate girl raised by nuns spending time with a seminus demon (sex demon) who wants to take her virginity to save his own life and that of his brothers (and the hospital)...interesting. Very interesting. Of course he finally becomes selfless and falls in love with a human who once she (ahem) does it, loses her immortality and charmed life bestowed upon her by angels. wowzers, what's a girl to do? She is almost raped by a fallen angel who is trying to bring about Armageddon, but he gets her necklace...but Wraith saves her virtue...only to have her give it to him so he can live to save the world. Which he does. And then he gets the girl...but she's dying now...hmm...what's a half-vampire to do? Oh, I know! Turn her...and he does and it's such a great HEA...Gem and Ky are finally together, and Reaver is back in Heaven and it's a great ending...except who is the new mysterious brother Lore? We shall see...</span>

  <span id="freeText11569508850628878676" style="display:none">This is one of my favorite PNR series and have read all the books - somehow I missed this one!!!!<br /><br />Wow, I adored Wraith...he's such a cool demon/vampire and sexy too...yes and a bit of a man..or should I say demon whore...until he meets Serena Kelley. <div id="review_59714890" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/59714890" />
    <a title="Eastofoz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz"><img alt="Eastofoz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1203907098p2/939365.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/59714890?book_show_action=true">Jun 15, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eastofoz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eastofoz" href="/user/show/939365-eastofoz">Eastofoz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of UF, Lara Adrian and Gina Showalter</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/939365-eastofoz?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/939365-eastofoz?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer59714890" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9398715464890707035">A no-go 2.5 star read for me. I don’t particularly like Urban Fantasy, but I do like romance and the romance in this story had virtually zero development, hardly any emotional investment for the reader or believability when it came to the “love” between Wraith and Serena. There are a few annoying sub-stories that went on for too long detracting from the main romance that bugged me too. The writing style reminds me of a cross between Lara Adrian’s <i>Midnight Breeds</i> and Gina Showalter’s <i>Lords of the</i></span>
  <span id="freeText9398715464890707035" style="display:none">A no-go 2.5 star read for me. I don’t particularly like Urban Fantasy, but I do like romance and the romance in this story had virtually zero development, hardly any emotional investment for the reader or believability when it came to the “love” between Wraith and Serena. There are a few annoying sub-stories that went on for too long detracting from the main romance that bugged me too. The writing style reminds me of a cross between Lara Adrian’s <i>Midnight Breeds</i> and Gina Showalter’s <i>Lords of the Underworld</i>.<br /><br />The hero, Wraith, is infected with a disease that's killing him and the only way to survive is by taking a charm that the heroine Serena has but to get the charm he has to have sex with her and if he does she dies. And then all the monsters pop up here and there to freak everyone out spreading an 'end of the world is nigh' vibe.<br /><br />The UF side of this book is well-done and the author provides a good glossary to help you understand the world she’s created so that you don’t get lost. You name the creature it’s in there. There are lots of mean, bad-ass ‘monsters’ all with their own agenda. Lots of chaos and gruesome violence, all very ‘vivid’ UF and if you look at it purely from that perspective it’s probably a good 4 stars. It’s marketed though as a paranormal romance novel which was why I read it and for me it couldn’t have fallen farther from the mark.<br /><br />I didn’t like the writing because it’s too harsh and silly expressions that just don’t work are thrown in pell mell. It’s as if the author tries to be funny or uses a dry kind humor but for me it came across as dumb and this is why the writing reminded me of Gina Showalter in some ways. You often get those stereotypical dumb guy sentences like <i>“Why didn’t you ever tell Serena you whipped up her baby batter”</i> or <i>“His stung pride put him on the hot side of pissed”</i> –seems even worse out of context but the whole book is peppered with this stuff which was why the writing style just didn’t do it for me. There is also nothing new here or nothing feels new in terms of love story. The ‘romance’ happens too fast. It’s more of lust-fest that suddenly morphs into a sappy “I love you. You are my life” that I couldn’t understand being that they never really did anything apart from jump each other and run away from the bad guys. <br /><br />Wraith is horribly crass, up in your face and borderline boorish. For a hot bad boy character he was a complete turn-off. Every few words is fuck this, fuck that, fuck it, fuck, fuck from pretty much everyone. It’s so overused that it loses its punch and starts to feel like a poor filler. Serena is all over the place. One minute she’s sane and normal and the next she’s all piss and vinegar mad; blows like the wind that one. Wraith is on her from the moment he meets her and she sort of likes it but then she pushes away but changes her mind and runs hot and cold. There’s no tension building. It’s as if they got it on all hot and heavy in the first 50 pages. Makes for a boring story for the remaining 350 pages. Sure there’s a lot sex and it’s quite descriptive but nothing held my interest. My mind kept wandering and I’d have to go back and reread parts. No investment in the characters. Jack-rabbits in heat 24/7 just don’t do it for me for a story. Poor character development, poor romance. The romance was almost secondary to the UF part of the story.<br /><br />I think you really have to like UF to enjoy this book and the romance aspect has to be secondary or an added bonus maybe. So I didn’t like this book, but this is not a bad thing --it’s just one less popular/growing series to add to the shelves ;)<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9398715464890707035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_92846974" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/92846974" />
    <a title="Leah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3050338-leah"><img alt="Leah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1474253068p2/3050338.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/92846974?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leah" href="/user/show/3050338-leah">Leah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Leah by: </span>
      Annie, Sam, Laurie, Alli, Gokce
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=adult-lit">adult-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3050338-leah?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer92846974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8478373875288146771">This book started out a little bit slow for me. Maybe because I jumped into it immediately upon finishing Desire Unchained, but I think it was more because I didn't immediately like or dislike Serena like I did Runa and Tayla, respectively. However, it didn't take me long to get into the story and fall for Wraith even more.<br/><br/>Wraith is quite possibly one of the sexiest demons out there. If Shade wasn't my favorite, Wraith would have immediately slid right into that spot. He is so strong yet vulnera</span>
  <span id="freeText8478373875288146771" style="display:none">This book started out a little bit slow for me. Maybe because I jumped into it immediately upon finishing Desire Unchained, but I think it was more because I didn't immediately like or dislike Serena like I did Runa and Tayla, respectively. However, it didn't take me long to get into the story and fall for Wraith even more.<br /><br />Wraith is quite possibly one of the sexiest demons out there. If Shade wasn't my favorite, Wraith would have immediately slid right into that spot. He is so strong yet vulnerable, cold yet loving, hard-hearted yet tender-hearted. He is so many contradictions combined that it's impossible not to love him. I mean, hell, he was going to die and let his brothers die so that he wouldn't have to kill Serena. He was willing to be tortured by the vampires so they would let him turn Serena. Does a guy get more devoted than that? I don't really think so. And I did like Serena, although it came on gradually. She was strong, brave, and intelligent but also sweet and loving, like our beloved Wraith. Her sacrifice for Wraith and humankind, giving up her charm and virginity, made me really like her, though. Although it sucked that she freaked out when she found out Wraith was a demon. But now they are together so I'm happy, and awww, there's a new baby Wraith on the scene!<br /><br />The biggest surprise of this book was definitely Lore. Holy shit, he is their brother! <i>He's Wraith, Shade, and Eidolon's brother.</i> I know I probably should have seen that one coming, but it totally blind sighted me. Wow. Yeah, still surprised.<br /><br />The sad thing is, I think I was more tortured by the situation with Kynan and Gem. Good Lord, those two drove me crazy with their back and forth when I just wanted them to <i>be together, damn it.</i> And I was going to hunt someone down and kill them if Ky and Gem's story had ended with Wraith draining him. No fucking way, Jose. I did not suffer through three books of their torturous relationship for it to end that way! And thank God Lore was able to bring Ky back. Now those two are living happily ever after and I couldn't be happier.<br /><br />The only thing that bothered me about this book was Serena calling Wraith "Josh." I wanted to smash my head against the wall every single time. And each time she called him that, it made me think of Mary calling Rhage "Hal" in Lover Eternal and how much I hated that. Bleck. Thank goodness she finally started calling him Wraith at the end.<br /><br />Anyway, this was, yet again, another great installment in the series and I don't think Wraith's story could have been any better.<br /><br />4.5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="8478373875288146771" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_554103369" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/554103369" />
    <a title="Lisa Kay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay"><img alt="Lisa Kay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534570690p2/2459470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/554103369?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>
      </span>

        rated it

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/10821627-passion-unleashed">review of another edition</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer554103369" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7513138554174501836"><i>Philae Island, Egypt, where the Temple of Isis is located. </i><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/>★★★★✩ (This is a review of the audiobook.) I was surprised to read some people didn't like the narrator, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2146135.Ren_e_Raudman' title='Renée Raudman' rel='nofollow noopener'>Renée Raudman</a>, as I thought she did a nice job. Although, I have only listened to the second book by another reader, not both, so that might have something to do with it. (Sometimes we audiobook aficionados get attached to a narrator doing a certain series.) <br/><br/>Ms. Raudman has a gravely, raspy voice that I thought went well </span>
  <span id="freeText7513138554174501836" style="display:none"><i>Philae Island, Egypt, where the Temple of Isis is located. </i><br><span>[image error]</span><br>★★★★✩ (This is a review of the audiobook.) I was surprised to read some people didn't like the narrator, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2146135.Ren_e_Raudman" title="Renée Raudman" rel="nofollow noopener">Renée Raudman</a>, as I thought she did a nice job. Although, I have only listened to the second book by another reader, not both, so that might have something to do with it. (Sometimes we audiobook aficionados get attached to a narrator doing a certain series.) <br><br>Ms. Raudman has a gravely, raspy voice that I thought went well with this story. Sort of like she’s speaking following a shot of whiskey on the rocks, after inhaling a bit of smoke in the air. She does get a little "breathy" at times, but for me, that lent an ambiance that fit the story-line.<br><br>In this third installment of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/375143.Larissa_Ione" title="Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">Larissa Ione</a>’s intriguing <i>Demonica</i> series Wraith has been poisoned by an assassin. In order to heal himself, he needs to find a Marked Sentinel named Serena Kelley, a human virgin who is charmed keeper of a certain necklace that protects her. The thing is, other than him swearing off humans, he’s got to make her give up her virginity, too; but in doing so, she will die. <br><br>As callous as this makes him, he has to consider the fate of others. Since he and his brothers have poured their blood, sweat, and tears into Underworld General Hospital, they are strongly tied into the place. Consequently, his health affects the building and its staff. So, he is off to Egypt to seduce Serena. I just love that setting for a romantic adventure, and there is plenty of action in this story.<br><br>I liked the world building and will certainly go on with the series that branch off from this one. The characters have a bit more layering this time around. Ms. Ione has a very creative imagination. I wondered if she had painted Wraith into a corner this time, but she manage to have him win me over surprisingly early, considering I didn't like him much in the first two books. Kudos!<br><br>P.S. The author has promised a much needed Glossary of Terms on her website, which would be a great help to audiobook listeners. Alas, as of this date it is not there.<br><br><i>
  <b>Update: March 23, 2013</b>
</i><br><br>Woohoo! I got a very nice post from the author, Ms. Larissa Ione. She directed me to the the glossary on her website: <blockquote>Just wanted to give you the link to the glossary of terms. It's actually the Demonica Compendium and is listed under "Free Reads" on my website. I'll see if I can add something on the site that makes it clearer! <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://larissaione.com/blog/books/#freereads">http://larissaione.com/blog/books/#fr...</a> </blockquote>Here is the book on GRs:<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13636496.The_Demonica_Compendium" title="The Demonica Compendium by Larissa Ione" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1336321429s/13636496.jpg" alt="The Demonica Compendium by Larissa Ione" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>
