<div id="review_53153704" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/53153704" />
    <a title="Corrine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2084774-corrine"><img alt="Corrine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461720592p2/2084774.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/53153704?book_show_action=true">Apr 18, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Corrine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Corrine" href="/user/show/2084774-corrine">Corrine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2084774-corrine?shelf=paranormal-fantasy-sci-fi-romance">paranormal-fantasy-sci-fi-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2084774-corrine?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2084774-corrine?shelf=deceitful-hero-or-heroine">deceitful-hero-or-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2084774-corrine?shelf=demon">demon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer53153704" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13605061500676984303">Okay, so Ione built up some really dark expectations of Wraith and failed to deliver, but IMO what we're left with is still the strongest in the series.<br/><br/>At the starting point of this book, half-demon half-vampire Wraith has already forced the 'sgenisis, the change all Seminus demons go through that makes them potent and gives them the unrelenting desire to impregnate females. However, it's not working like he thought it would; he thought it was make him a sex-craving animal with no human conscien</span>
  <span id="freeText13605061500676984303" style="display:none">Okay, so Ione built up some really dark expectations of Wraith and failed to deliver, but IMO what we're left with is still the strongest in the series.<br /><br />At the starting point of this book, half-demon half-vampire Wraith has already forced the 'sgenisis, the change all Seminus demons go through that makes them potent and gives them the unrelenting desire to impregnate females. However, it's not working like he thought it would; he thought it was make him a sex-craving animal with no human conscience or emotions, but for some reason, though he craves sex, he's basically still the same. Until he finds out that he has been poisoned by a toxin that has no cure, and unless he obtains a certain charm, he will die. The problem is that the charm is being held by a human female, and to obtain it, he has to seduce her virginity away from her. Because of past traumas in his life, Wraith considers human females off limits, <i>especially</i> virgin ones. But when he finds out that his life force is tied to the existence of Underworld General, and therefore his brothers' as well, Wraith is willing to take one for the team.<br /><br />The carrier of the charm, Serena Kelley, has something else in mind. Although she's wildly attracted to who she thinks is no one more than a fellow treasure hunter, she can never know sexual intimacy in its fullest, because to do so would cause the disease she contracted as a child to progress and eventually kill her. <br /><br />As Wraith goes back and forth with pushing forward in his plan to seduce Serena or not, he begins to find out just why his brothers would be crazy enough to take a mate,and how hard it is to choose between your own personal happiness and the well-being of your family and friends. <br /><br />In reality, Wraith gave in much quicker than I thought he would, and with much less angst, which just made me like him more. And Serena showed a selflessness that was on par with Madeline from Garwood's <b>Honour's Splendor</b> (sp? I know one is spelled with a "u"in the title). A good conclusion to an interesting trilogy, although I was bummed by the quick resultion of Kynan &amp; Gem, and am not at all looking forward to any book featuring Seminus assassin Lore, should Ione choose to write. B</span>
  <a data-text-id="13605061500676984303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/140254889?book_show_action=true">Jan 12, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-i-wanna-hug">hero-i-wanna-hug</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-hot-male-in-my-harem">hero-hot-male-in-my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-larissa-ione">author-larissa-ione</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer140254889" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5225051057614403570"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><br/>Wraith is dying. The only way he can save himself is to find a charm, but to do this he must first seduce and take the virginty of a human woman, a human woman who will die without the charm. After being tortured by his insane mother, human women have been off the menu, both sexually and as a meal, but more is at stake then just Wraith's live and so he goes hunting for Serena. But can he really do it, especially when he thinks he is starting to fall in love with the spunky, fearless hum</span>
  <span id="freeText5225051057614403570" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br /><br />Wraith is dying. The only way he can save himself is to find a charm, but to do this he must first seduce and take the virginty of a human woman, a human woman who will die without the charm. After being tortured by his insane mother, human women have been off the menu, both sexually and as a meal, but more is at stake then just Wraith's live and so he goes hunting for Serena. But can he really do it, especially when he thinks he is starting to fall in love with the spunky, fearless human? <br /><br />This one is definitely my favourite in the series so far. Wraith is a great hero, a complete bad boy who excels at two things, fighting and sex and seems to not care about much else, apart from maybe his brothers. In this book, we get to see a different side to Wraith as he starts falling in love with Serena, and as he gets more tender and protective he becomes the biggest danger to a womas heart, a bad boy with a heart.<br /><br />What I also liked about this one was the progression of the story line, it had a strong plot driving the story and I wanted to see the resolution of that as well as Wraith and Serena's HEA. I also liked the continuation of Gem and Kylan's romance, I love it when books have a secondary romance, and this one was particularly good, and I have enjoyed watching it develop thorughout the last three books.<br /><br />We also had the introduction of a new brother! Lore, and I go on to reading about him next, Ione left some intriguig hints about him and where he comes from and what he is doing, I can't wait to read more. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5225051057614403570" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_369314955" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karolina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karolina" href="/user/show/9788746-karolina">Karolina</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9788746-karolina?shelf=hot-and-steamy">hot-and-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9788746-karolina?shelf=broken-soul">broken-soul</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer369314955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4938232134002553207">I wanted to give this book five stars I really, really did. I loved the story, dilemma, all the twists and turns Ione can catch you off guard with but what I was missing was Wraith! As I'm quite worked up I'm going to pass on recapping the details of the actual story and I'm going to focus on the issues that's bothering me.<br/><br/>The build up to Wraith's story in the first two books was great, so unsurprisingly my expectations were high, the whole story definitely did not disappoint, what did disappoin</span>
  <span id="freeText4938232134002553207" style="display:none">I wanted to give this book five stars I really, really did. I loved the story, dilemma, all the twists and turns Ione can catch you off guard with but what I was missing was Wraith! As I'm quite worked up I'm going to pass on recapping the details of the actual story and I'm going to focus on the issues that's bothering me.<br /><br />The build up to Wraith's story in the first two books was great, so unsurprisingly my expectations were high, the whole story definitely did not disappoint, what did disappoint was the guy who suppose to be Wraith! The Wraith who's possessed with insatiable lust and madness, who's soul is so tormented he scares everyone with his look, the Wraith who don't give a shit about anyone but inside is scared to care, the Wraith who needed to fight his past demons really hard to come out on the other side! What I got was a mellow version of the most broken and haunted character I was expecting. I feel cheated. I do understand his life has changed since he's been poisoned and going to die, but I felt like it was to easy for him to flirt, charm and care for Serena knowing how much he hates women. Especially since we learn his real past and let me tell you things he's been through don't disappear in a matter of days. Shade's story and his inner battle now seems a lot more powerful than Wraith's, and it suppose to be the other way around.<br /><br />In previous story I found Gem and Kym's relationship really interesting but here they got on my nerves quite a few time. Especially Gem, she's been in love with the guy for years while he's been married, now that he's available and wants her she pushes him away. Come on girl, make up you mind!<br /><br /><br />Never the less the action, dilemma, great characters and off the wall humor made me sail through the book in a day. I still really enjoyed it. I think Ione has a great talent of making the readers love the characters despite the fact that they can be really disturbing and flawed. I might have a little break from Demonica for now, but will definitely return to finish the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4938232134002553207" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText6738418793003898189" style="display:none">This book was much more plausible for me. Both characters were developed, full and layered, and they did suit each other. I understood both of them; their conflicts were touching and they were very real characters, rather than archetypes. They were both likable, especially Wraith, who's really a big softy and an ideal vampire when he's not, LOL. ;)<br /><br />I think it helps when the conflict is from without, not from within the relationship because otherwise it's easy to get into contrived land. The action plot was excellently executed too- it flowed very well; there was no confusion, etc. and the villain was truly dastardly.<br /><br />It also felt less rushed and there was less eye-rolling dialogue (inner and outer). Ione worried less about trying to make him come off as smart-alecky and more as a serious character. Overall, I liked this one better than the second (she's been redeemed), and I'm looking forward to the next. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14152179087923483713"> <b>Another fantastic book.</b><br/><br/>I absolutely loved this book. There was so much going on and I enjoyed every page of it.<br/> Okay, so I'll give you a quick <i>run-down</i> of the story... Wraith has been injection with a fatal dose of poison by an assassin, courtesy of Roag (yeah, I know he's dead. You'll have to read it to see what I'm talking about) *evil laughs* ;)<br/> Serena is a treasure hunter, like Wraith, who was <i>charmed</i> by Angels. She is the Keeper of a very important Amulet. Said Amulet/Charm stops Serena fr</span>
  <span id="freeText14152179087923483713" style="display:none"> <b>Another fantastic book.</b><br /><br />I absolutely loved this book. There was so much going on and I enjoyed every page of it.<br /> Okay, so I'll give you a quick <i>run-down</i> of the story... Wraith has been injection with a fatal dose of poison by an assassin, courtesy of Roag (yeah, I know he's dead. You'll have to read it to see what I'm talking about) *evil laughs* ;)<br /> Serena is a treasure hunter, like Wraith, who was <i>charmed</i> by Angels. She is the Keeper of a very important Amulet. Said Amulet/Charm stops Serena from being hurt and grants her immortality. This Charm is Wraith's last chance at survival. The catch? The Charm can only be transferred to Wraith if she willingly gives him... <i>*drum roll please*</i>... her virginity.<br /> I know, it sounds a little cheesy but I promise you, it works.<br /><br /> Serena is amazing. I really loved her character and the way she has embraced the gift the Amulet gives her. She totally kicks demon arse whenever the opportunity arises. LOL<br /> She is beautiful, selfless and caring. I loved the way she always took care of Wraith, she shows him a relationship that he has never even dreamed of, one of trust, admiration, affection and tenderness. It was beautiful to watch them together.<br /><br /> Wraith is my favourite hero of the series so far. Once he is away from everyone else, he isn't worrying about what he looks like or what other people think of him. He lets the new emotions he feels for Serena fill his heart. He looks after her, protects her and desires her. <br /> I really liked seeing him deal with all the new feelings...<br /><br /> <i>"I love Italy." ...Her smile grew dreamy, and he really wished she wouldn't do that, because it made him want to kiss her.<br /> Which was crazy, because he'd never kissed a female before, not in his hundred years of life. But suddenly he wanted to put his mouth on Serena's and see what all the fuss was about.'</i><br /> <br /><br /> Another thing I love about this series is the fact that there are many secondary story lines that run alongside the main plot. <br /> There is now the added story of the Angel's and the Fallen, which was incredible, by the way. There are keys between Heaven and Hell (Sheoul), updates on previous characters and the introduction of new ones.<br /><br /> Which brings me to Lore. I was absolutely enthralled by this guy. I don't know what it is, maybe the fact that we don't know much about him yet, <i>(not telling you the big secret, my lips are sealed. LOL)</i> other than the fact that he's incredibly sexy, he's an enslaved assassin being used by a demon, and everything that comes into contact with his hand, dies.<br /> <i>'Accidently killing a partner he liked during sex wasn't something he wanted to repeat. Killing one during sex that he'd been pain to eliminate... That was a little different.'</i><br /> I cannot wait to learn more about this guy.<br /><br /> We get to see Kynan and Gem working some things out and an Angel prophecy that Kynan is involved with. I am really excited about what could happen between them in the future.<br /><br /> Really loving this series and cannot wait to read the next book.<br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="14152179087923483713" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_2173230315" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2173230315" />
    <a title="Siobhan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35855553-siobhan"><img alt="Siobhan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1510311895p2/35855553.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2173230315?book_show_action=true">Nov 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Siobhan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Siobhan" href="/user/show/35855553-siobhan">Siobhan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/16102796-passion-unleashed">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2173230315" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3732561919181239136">Passion Unleashed is the third book in the Demonica series, and I’ve been so excited for this one throughout the two prior books. I loved both Pleasure Unbound and Desire Unchained, falling in love with the characters. Yet I couldn’t wait to read Wraith’s story. I’m a sucker for tortured heroes and whilst he was never my favourite of the brothers, I had high hopes for his story.<br/><br/>Although I did enjoy this one, it wasn't quite as mind blowing as I'd been hoping for considering my interest in the ma</span>
  <span id="freeText3732561919181239136" style="display:none">Passion Unleashed is the third book in the Demonica series, and I’ve been so excited for this one throughout the two prior books. I loved both Pleasure Unbound and Desire Unchained, falling in love with the characters. Yet I couldn’t wait to read Wraith’s story. I’m a sucker for tortured heroes and whilst he was never my favourite of the brothers, I had high hopes for his story.<br /><br />Although I did enjoy this one, it wasn't quite as mind blowing as I'd been hoping for considering my interest in the main character. You see, my expectations for Wraith were high. His story was a lot of fun, I cannot deny that, but the whole tortured hero element left a lot to be desired. There was so much build-up throughout the first two books, that I expected my heart to be ripped into pieces when I finally got to read Wraith’s story. Some elements were dark, as I had hoped, but it was not up to my usual tortured hero standard.<br /><br />Despite feeling somewhat let down by Wraith’s background, I did enjoy this one a lot. Things have been building throughout the first two books, and we finally got to witness as a lot of things came together. I’m never quite sure where Larissa Ione is going to take us next, and in this one she delivered another multi-layered story. Whilst this can work as a standalone novel for the romantic elements, I would recommend reading this series in order if you wish to understand all the references made throughout as there is a lot going on.<br /><br />In addition to being given Wraith’s story, we see the continuous storyline from the prior books – the Gem and Ky arc – come to a head. Although there were times when I felt as though their storyline was taking the attention away from Wraith, I came to understand why it was given so much attention by the end of the book. In addition, we also get introduced to new characters that will be important in the future books. Whilst there were times when I felt like too much was going on, and times where I wished the attention would shift to other characters, it really did come together so well in the end. It wasn’t at all the story I had been anticipating, but I did enjoy it a lot.<br /><br />Having read through the first three books in rapid succession, there’s no doubt about my addiction to the series. As soon as I finished Passion Unleashed I grabbed Ecstasy Unveiled, needing even more of this series. Whilst I’d expected I would enjoy this series, I never expected to find myself quite as addicted as I am. I think it’s safe to say, Larissa Ione has managed to wiggle her way onto my favourite authors list with this series, and as soon as I’m done powering through the Demonica books I’m going to have to look at her other series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3732561919181239136" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

In order to get the charm he will be the reason she dies! Oh and top it of .. Armageddon is kinda happening! How great is it if the author can sell a underworld hospital to you and you actually BUY IT! <br /><br />I was sold! Like “take all my money because I will buy the rest of this series”-sold. <br /><br />Getting inside Wraith head was epic. Learning what happened to him as a child was so heartbreaking and you really understands why he is such an ASS! #alphaassholesArethebest<br /><br />And Serena. A woman with an adventures bone in her body! Loved it! <br />And the sacrifice she made. BEAUTIFUL! Love going on adventures, and for her to love that too. #bonding #same<br /><br />Read: 17/03/2018<br />1st rating: 5 Stars <br />Genre/sub-genres: urban fantasy/vampires/demons/paranormal/romance<br />Cover: 3 Stars <br />Will I recommend: STUPID question because damn well I will!   <span id="freeText212399168300664380" style="display:none">Wow! The title speaks for itself.The love and passion unleashed between partners, family, friends, and saving the world, was so surreal and amazing! There was more than enough love to spread around and make everyone mushy, yet strong for one another. Wraith &amp; Serena, Gem &amp; Ky , two new couples added to this wonderful series which made this novel remarkable! I'm more than amazed and awed. I didn't even know I finished until I realized I was reading about the author, Just comes to show it was a wonderful story, and I had wished it didn't end!<br /><br />My happy thoughts &amp; thanks goes out to all my wonderful GR friends who recommended &amp; pushed me to read this series.   function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OixIHgydurKGh6Hg1qR2y2S8ITBmvn/uRgvK6MHjVwKOenLap2Tn5axmf6VldQme0Gk9xqWxS/V7vHc5TbZlCA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('qVQ/6Nellu2g15xP4j2wke6ezrQZAXla2vLBmbDiDJodAgUsfFzLuoo2QgpR7M/EWkvSQtoOTUHnRXxIPLc+kA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer8668860353220468728">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would n</span>
  <span id="freeText8668860353220468728" style="display:none">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would never be caught without a bottle of Champagne chilling in the fridge…just in case. She currently lives in Wisconsin with her retired U.S. Coast Guard husband, her son, a rescue cat named Vegas, and her very own hellhounds, a King Shepherd named Hexe and a Belgian Malinois named Duvel.</span>

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_19265916').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_19265916').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_19265916').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
